Or that he or she would be more confident about themselves? We want to help your child to develop communication, language and social-emotional skills through highly interactive and engaging drama activities. 													<img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="800" height="459" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-Objectives-01-1024x588.jpg" class="attachment-large size-large wp-image-10713" alt="" srcset="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-Objectives-01-1024x588.jpg 1024w, https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-Objectives-01-300x172.jpg 300w, https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-Objectives-01-768x441.jpg 768w, https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-Objectives-01-1536x882.jpg 1536w, https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-Objectives-01-2048x1176.jpg 2048w, https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-Objectives-01-600x345.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px">													</div>

			<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Our Approach</h2>		</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5ee84dd elementor-widget elementor-widget-elementor-custom-table" data-id="5ee84dd" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="elementor-custom-table.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
			
        <div class="table-container">

            <table class="tafe-table">

                
                <thead class="tafe-table-header">

                <tr>

                    <th class="elementor-inline-editing elementor-repeater-item-3194e68">No.</th><th class="elementor-inline-editing elementor-repeater-item-7dfab01">Approach	</th><th class="elementor-inline-editing elementor-repeater-item-13e4e63">Description</th>
                </tr>

                </thead>

                
                <tbody class="tafe-table-body">

                <tr>

                    <td class="elementor-repeater-item-039a1af"><p>1.</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-77c3005"><p>Language-based</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-2b1ae91"><p>The exposure to different texts increases our students' appreciation for the English language.</p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-73c1594"><p>2.</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-64cffdc">Direct &amp; Explicit	</td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-38cc5c5">Recognizing that students with learning difficulties will require direct and explicit instructions. One-on-one support, additional guidance, and tailored strategies are provided to help them succeed.
</td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-44e95ad"><p>3.</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-36fd558">Cognitive</td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-20a2c34">Drama activities are cognitive in nature as they engage various mental processes and stimulate cognitive development. Examples include creative story writing, roleplay, improvisation, memorization of scripts, rehearsing, and performing.
</td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-0660d50"><p>4.</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-aa4578a">Diagnostic &amp; Prescriptive	</td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-087de80">Drama teachers regularly assess students' abilities and adapt activities based on the class dynamics.
</td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-2b0ae91"><p>5.</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-4bea928">Structure, Cumulative &amp; Sequential, but Flexible</td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-2612d37">The curriculum progresses from easy to complex concepts, with flexibility to support the integration of previously learned skills based on students' abilities.
</td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-c0f2563"><p>6.</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-1e93a99">Multi-sensory	</td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-739a67e">Multisensory learning is integral to the drama class. It engages students through the use of stage and hand props and the presentation of skills that combine multiple senses, such as visual and aural cues.</td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-7440e0a"><p>7.</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-75fa5ac">Emotionally Sound	</td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-e71b54e">Drama teachers are trained in the field of special learning needs, with a better understanding of students' strengths and weaknesses.</td>
                </tr>

                </tbody>

            </table>

        </div>

			<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Recommended for</h2>		</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6e381208 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="6e381208" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
							<p>The Speech and Drama Arts Programme is recommended to students who want to explore the learning of the English language through drama skills and aspire to be confident communicators who are great team players and able to think creatively.</p>						</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6b62d7a elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="6b62d7a" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
			<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The programme caters to different age groups</h2>		</div>
				</div>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
							<ul><li>Creative Drama (K2 – Primary 3)</li><li>Literacy Through Drama Programme (Primary 4 – Primary 6)</li><li>Educational Drama (Secondary 1 – Secondary 2)</li></ul>						</div>
				</div>

							<ul><li>K2, all primary and lower secondary school students</li><li>No formal diagnosis of dyslexia is required</li><li>Open to non-DAS students</li></ul>						</div>

                    <td class="elementor-repeater-item-37317c9"><p><strong>COMPREHENSION</strong><br>By Amrit Kaur Gill</p><p>Drama Activities can add an element of fun to reading comprehension. With drama activities, it provides an opportunity for students to engage with text in an interactive manner. By doing this, it helps to develops students’ comprehension skills in a fun and non-pressurising manner. In this article, we explore three drama activities that you can try out with your child or student!</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/drama-and-learning-comprehension/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-b8f44af"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/pasted-image-0.jpg" alt="SDA 0303 web" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-2ca1f60"><p><strong>DRAMA, A DIFFERENT WAY TO LEARN.</strong><br>By Corinne Ang</p><p>Most people do not associate drama with learning.&nbsp;This subject has the reputation of being fun and loud, which might seem counter-productive to some. However, a deeper look uncovers its ability to enhance speaking, listening, comprehension and critical thinking skills. In this article, we explore how learning drama can contribute positively to an individual academically and personally.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/drama-a-different-way-to-learn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-67c06b3"><p><img decoding="async" class="alignnone" style="display: block; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA_0303-web.jpg" alt="SDA 0303 web" width="1773" height="1182"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-ce693aa"><p><strong>IMPROV TO IMPROVE</strong><br>By Amrit Kaur Gill</p><p>Improvisation provides the opportunity for an individual to develop one’s self on various levels. With improv exercises and engaging activities, individuals will be taught to think and react on the spot. This will help the individual to learn how to cope with uncertainties. Find out how improv helps with learning!</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/improv-to-improve/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-c6454b4"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/smiling-girl-with-crown-her-head-peeking-from-red-curtain-small.png" alt="smiling girl with crown her head peeking from red curtain small" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-80c8b46"><p><strong>MAKING THE SOCIAL-EMOTIONAL CONNECTIONS WITH DRAMA</strong><br>By Corinne Ang</p><p>Being able to manage one’s emotions and navigate social interactions are essential skills for all children. An argument can be made that children with dyslexia require these skills even more.&nbsp;Drama is an excellent tool to introduce and sustain social-emotional competencies. As an art form, it is greatly associated with human interaction.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/making-the-social-emotional-connections-with-drama/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-0488898"><p><img decoding="async" style="margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; display: block;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDAimage4.png" alt="SDAimage4" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-9d5d727"><p><strong>TWEENS AND TEENS - THE FRUSTRATION IS REAL!</strong><br>By Muzdalifah Hamzah</p><p>Tweens and teens are at the stage where they are overly consumed by the changes in their bodies and the social world.&nbsp;What can parents do to help their tweens and teens?</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/tweens-and-teens-the-frustration-is-real/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-8ef2ae6"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/teen.jpg" alt="teen" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-561f32a"><p><strong>The Effectiveness of using Drama as a Tool to build Social-Emotional Development of Children with Dyslexia in Singapore</strong><br>By Muzdalifah Hamzah</p><p>This study explores the efficacy of a speech and drama programme in developing social-emotional literacy of children with dyslexia.</p><p>View on YouTube&nbsp;<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lHBUPpm71vE" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-ce687d0"><p><iframe title="YouTube video player" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/lHBUPpm71vE" width="100%" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen"></iframe></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-b9afb81"><p><strong>Dyslexia and Drama in Education</strong><br>By Pushpaa Arumugam and Muzdalifah Hamzah</p><p>This recording is a presentation from UNITE SpLD conference in 2016.</p><p>View on YouTube&nbsp;<a href="https://youtu.be/10cvIHixQPM" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-44c27df"><p><iframe title="YouTube video player" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/10cvIHixQPM" width="100%" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen"></iframe></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-258cc98"><p><strong>HELP! I AM TEACHING DRAMA ONLINE!</strong><br>By Muzdalifah Hamzah</p><p>Being a drama instructor in Speech &amp; Drama Arts (SDA) programme, it didn’t occur to me that one day I will teach drama online. A typical drama class would involve a lot of movement activities, role-playing with friends, voice exercises and rehearsals after rehearsals in a big space. “How to teach drama online?” And a lot more questions ran in my head.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/SDA-2.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-d2d335b"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/24273623_1462578053789426_8490150162198792974_o.jpg" alt="24273623 1462578053789426 8490150162198792974 o" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-743a64f"><p><strong>HOW CAN SPEECH AND DRAMA CLASS HELP MY CHILD?</strong><br>By&nbsp;DAS Speech &amp; Drama Arts Team</p><p>Contrary to popular parents’ perception, a speech and drama class is more than just role-playing and acting. It nurtures imagination and creativity in a way that it cannot be learned but through experience. Speech and drama classes like the one offered in das can be that powerful tool to help children, especially those with learning differences. Let us explore some of the ways a speech &amp; drama class can help your child.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/SDA-1.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-8f597b1"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA7.jpg" alt="SDA7" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td>

						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6e381208 elementor-widget__width-initial elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="6e381208" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
							<div class="description"><p>The Speech and Drama Arts programme provides children with SpLDs a safe platform to learn to express themselves, experience teamwork and develop their confidence. Understanding the background and characteristics of these students has allowed us to develop a programme that would enhance their learning journey and discover their potential.</p><p><strong>Our Approach:</strong></p><p>The aim of the SES Speech and Drama Arts Programme is to develop literacy, communication and presentation skills and boost the self-esteem of learners with dyslexia. Drama can be a powerful tool to help students with learning differences to experience language learning in a fun way.</p><p><strong>Drama Workshops for Schools:</strong></p><p>At the das, we conduct SES Speech and Drama workshops for students both in primary and secondary schools. Our school workshops are customised to meet the demands of our clients, in order to achieve the school’s desired objectives and outcomes.</p><p><strong>Our Instructors:</strong></p><ul><li>Trained educational therapists to support students with dyslexia.</li><li>Trained in teaching Speech and Drama classes</li><li>MOE registered instructors</li></ul><p><strong>Drama &amp; Learning:</strong></p><p>Most people do not associate drama with learning.<br>A deeper look uncovers its ability to enhance speaking, listening, comprehension and critical thinking skills. In the various articles in the link below, one can explore how learning drama can contribute positively to an individual academically and personally.&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/services/programmes/speech-and-drama-arts/#drama-learning" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Click on the link to read more about it!</a></p><p><strong>Gallery</strong></p><p><a href="/services/programmes/speech-and-drama-arts.html#gallery" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Check out our gallery page</a>&nbsp;to catch our SES Speech and Drama Arts students in action!</p><p><strong>Contact Us:</strong></p><p>For general enquiries and to find out more&nbsp;about Speech &amp; Drama Arts workshop in your&nbsp;school, please contact :</p><p><a href="https://www.das.org.sg/about-das/about-us/staff-directory/staff/6-anaberta-oehlers-jaen" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Anaberta Oehlers-Jaen</a><br>Email:&nbsp;<a href="mailto:anaberta@das.org.sg">anaberta@das.org.sg</a></p></div>						</div>

                    </tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-8471f8e"><p><strong>STUDENT SPOTLIGHT – TANIECIA</strong><br>By Muzdalifah Hamzah</p><p>Taniecia has a bubbly personality and is currently the President of the Student Council in her school. She enjoys organising school activities and plays netball as a CCA. No one would have guessed that this 15-year-old girl once struggled in class and had a hard time accepting that she had dyslexia.</p><p>Read Taniecia's story <a href="https://das.org.sg/student-spotlight-taniecia-lau/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-b61c452"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone" style="display: block;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/taniecia3.png" alt="Rizqah 01" width="2560" height="2560"></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-8e79f30"><p><strong>STUDENT SPOTLIGHT – HAZEL</strong><br>By Corinne Ang</p><p>Hazel Low joined the Speech and Drama Arts (SDA) programme in October 2021. She was just nine then. Hazel has a great work ethic and exhibits a positive outlook in life. Big or small, she portrayed every role with the same enthusiasm and earnestness. Each production she undertook came with its own set of challenges she had to overcome.</p><p>Read Hazel's story <a href="https://das.org.sg/hazel-low-speech-drama-arts-spotlight/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-fb24103"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone" style="display: block;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/Hazel1-295x200.png" alt="Rizqah 01" width="2560" height="2560"></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-fbb4848"><p><strong>TESTIMONIAL FOR MS MUZDALIFAH</strong><br>By Mr Yong, Parent</p><p>“Dear Miss Muzdalifah ,</p><p>I wanted to take a moment to express my heartfelt appreciation for your dedication and hard work in teaching das CLASS Drama and Speech. Your commitment to ensuring that each and every student in the class receives a quality education is truly inspiring.”</p><p>Read the full testimonial&nbsp;<a href="https://www.das.org.sg/services/about-our-services/testimonials" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>.</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-22dc5e4"><p><img decoding="async" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-gala-1-min.jpg" alt="SDA gala 1" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-810d78b"><p><strong>SDA PERFORMANCE AT SGAA 2022</strong><br>By&nbsp;Amrit Kaur Gill</p><p>On 26 November 2022, SDA students from both Bishan and Bedok Learning Centre presented an original piece - Castaway, at the DAS Student Graduation &amp; Achievement Awards Ceremony 2022. Castaway is a tale of four children who were stranded on an island after a sea storm.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/lights-drama-action-speech-and-drama-arts-performance-for-sgaa-2022/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-d0afa3a"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/IMG_8188.webp" alt="IMG 8188" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-0777be8"><p><strong>SDA PERFORMANCE AT DAS30 CHARITY GALA DINNER</strong><br>By Corinne Ang</p><p>On 7 September 2022, eight students from the DAS Speech and Drama Arts programme graced the das 30th Anniversary Charity Gala Dinner with a drama &amp; dance performance. This performance was the first live show done by the drama class since the circuit breaker in 2020.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/sda-performance-at-das-30th-anniversary-charity-gala-dinner/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-17cd67f"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/305459700_5310070079040185_4896576011289780470_n-min.jpg" alt="305459700 5310070079040185 4896576011289780470 n" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-5197ce5"><p><strong>STUDENT SPOTLIGHT – RIZQAH</strong><br>By Corinne Ang</p><p>Rizqah joined the Speech and Drama Arts (SDA) programme in September 2021, when she was seven years old. Despite enjoying drama activities, she was initially very shy. Rizqah has since grown in confidence after joining the programme.</p><p>Read Rizqah’s story&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/speech-drama-arts-student-spotlight-rizqah/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-268e26b"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Rizqah-01-min-scaled.jpg" alt="Rizqah 01" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-63d3361"><p><strong>STUDENT SPOTLIGHT – ZIQRY</strong><br>By Muzdalifah Hamzah</p><p>Ziqry joined the DAS Speech &amp; Drama Arts Programme when he was only 9 years old. As a drama student, Ziqry always gives his best in class and in performances. He looks forward to performances and enjoys the limelight whenever he’s on the stage.</p><p>Read Ziqry’s story&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/speech-drama-arts-student-spotlight-ziqry/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-c67342a"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/student-spotlight-ziqry-01-min-scaled.jpg" alt="student spotlight ziqry 01" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-08cd120"><p><strong>SDA VIRTUAL SHOWCASE 2021</strong><br>By Amrit Kaur Gill</p><p>On 28 December 2021, 36 of our Speech and Drama Arts (SDA) students adorned the screens for the Virtual DAS Showcase. The SDA students from two DAS Learning Centres (Bedok and Bishan), aged between 6-15 years old presented various plays for their parents and for their teacher’s DAS.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/sda-virtual-showcase-2021/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-91f99c8"><img decoding="async" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/SDA-SHOWCASE-2021-crop-min.jpg" alt="SDA SHOWCASE 2021 crop" width="100%" height="NaN"></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-386a211"><p><strong>THE SHOW MUST GO ON</strong><br>By Corinne Ang</p><p>What comes to mind when you think of a drama class? Chances are, it will be a group of children, in a classroom acting out a scene. As drama teachers, these images are etched in our minds. However, in the last term, our drama classes took a different form. Students entered class by literally popping up in little boxes lined up on computer screens. Suddenly, sound quality and internet connection became a concern and information was shared with a single click. Students and teachers alike had to relearn how to function in this new environment.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/the-show-must-go-on/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-f154160"><p><img decoding="async" style="display: block;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/better_tomorrow-min.jpg" alt="better tomorrow" width="100%" height="NaN"></p></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-d756de2"><p><strong>3…2…1…ACTION!</strong><br>By Amrit Kaur Gill</p><p>The Speech and Drama Arts (SDA) team recognises speech and drama as an effective means of developing our students’ talents and self-confidence, which in turn can lead to a more positive self-concept for our students. Despite being in a pandemic, it didn’t deter the Speech and Drama Arts team from putting up a performance.</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/321action/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-eb3ad4e"><img decoding="async" style="display: block;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/gruffalo-min.png" alt="gruffalo" width="100%" height="NaN"></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-df9cf61"><p><strong>ACTORS ASSEMBLE! WE ARE BACK IN CLASS!</strong><br>By Corinne Ang</p><p>“It’s good to come back because I can see my friends’ real faces and not from the screen.”</p><p>Despite the new routines and challenges, students are happy to be reunited. Let’s hear what they had to say!</p><p>View the article&nbsp;<a href="https://das.org.sg/actors-assemble-we-are-back-in-class/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>!</p></td><td class="elementor-repeater-item-b267d34"><img decoding="async" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Speech and Drama Arts" src="https://das.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/sda-bishan5-min.jpg" alt="sda bishan5" width="100%" height="NaN"></td></tr><tr><td class="elementor-repeater-item-8782448"><p><strong>NOAH YAP – ASPIRING ACTOR</strong><br>AN INTERVIEW WITH NOAH YAP BY THE SPEECH AND DRAMA ARTS TEAM</p><p>Noah Yap, a 12-year-old cheerful and diligent student, has been in the Speech and Drama Arts (SDA) programme at Dyslexia Association of Singapore (das) for the past 2.5 years. After being in the programme for some time, Noah decided to continue his passion for Theatre Arts in Secondary School.</p><p>SDA sat down with Noah over some biscuits to gain an insight into his life as SDA student and the decisions he made. 					<section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-196489ab elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="196489ab" data-element_type="section">
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-20ef8c00" data-id="20ef8c00" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-f145fc2 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="f145fc2" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
			<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS</h2>		</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c9adbaf elementor-widget elementor-widget-toggle" data-id="c9adbaf" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="toggle.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
			<style>.elementor-toggle{text-align:left}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title{font-weight:700;line-height:1;margin:0;padding:15px;border-bottom:1px solid #d5d8dc;cursor:pointer;outline:none}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title .elementor-toggle-icon{display:inline-block;width:1em}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title .elementor-toggle-icon svg{margin-inline-start:-5px;width:1em;height:1em}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title .elementor-toggle-icon.elementor-toggle-icon-right{float:right;text-align:right}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title .elementor-toggle-icon.elementor-toggle-icon-left{float:left;text-align:left}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title .elementor-toggle-icon .elementor-toggle-icon-closed{display:block}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title .elementor-toggle-icon .elementor-toggle-icon-opened{display:none}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title.elementor-active{border-bottom:none}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title.elementor-active .elementor-toggle-icon-closed{display:none}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title.elementor-active .elementor-toggle-icon-opened{display:block}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-content{padding:15px;border-bottom:1px solid #d5d8dc;display:none}@media (max-width:540px){.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-title{padding:12px}.elementor-toggle .elementor-tab-content{padding:12px 10px}}.e-con-inner>.elementor-widget-toggle,.e-con>.elementor-widget-toggle{width:var(--container-widget-width);--flex-grow:var(--container-widget-flex-grow)}</style>		<div class="elementor-toggle">
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2111" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="1" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2111" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">1. What is the aim of the Speech and Drama Arts (SDA) Programme?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2111" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="1" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2111"><p>The main aim of the SDA Programme is to provide an outlet for students to express themselves, ideas and thoughts without inhibition. The Speech and Drama Arts Programme focuses on developing acting skills, language skills and social-emotional skills through highly interactive and engaging drama activities.</p></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2112" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="2" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2112" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">2. What is covered in the programme?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2112" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="2" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2112"><p>These are the components covered in our SDA Programme:</p><ol><li>Introduction to Drama – What is Drama (story, scenes, settings, characters, dialogues)</li><li>Tableaux (Freeze frames)</li><li>Mime</li><li>Emotions</li><li>Voice Expression</li><li>Physical Expression</li><li>Critical Thinking</li><li>Language development through the exposure of different text types</li></ol></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2113" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="3" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2113" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">3. How are the lessons at the DAS different from what is offered at tuition/enrichment centres?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2113" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="3" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2113"><p>The SDA Programme is designed such that students participate in both guided and self-directed activities that engages them kinaesthetically and cognitively. The activities facilitated during lessons encourage affective aspects of reading and literacy while offering multiple opportunities for meaningful communication, social interaction, discussion and feedback. The teachers also have the ability to understand the needs of a child with dyslexia as they are trained Educational Therapists.</p></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2114" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="4" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2114" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">4. How many students are there in a class?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2114" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="4" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2114"><p>Each SDA class has a maximum of 10 students and a minimum of 6 students. The big class size allows students to work together in a team for presentations.</p></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2115" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="5" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2115" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">5. Does the SDA programme offer one-to-one remediation?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2115" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="5" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2115"><p>No, we do not offer one-to-one remediation.</p></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2116" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="6" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2116" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">6. How much is the SDA Programme?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2116" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="6" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2116"><p>Please refer to all our Programme Fees&nbsp;<a href="https://demowebsg2.com/services/about-our-services/all-programme-fees.html">here</a><strong><br></strong></p><p dir="ltr">Lessons are charged on a termly basis (10 lessons), inclusive of GST.<strong>&nbsp;Bursary is available</strong>, including for a second Specialised Educational Services (SES) programme.</p><p dir="ltr"><strong>For example:</strong><br>Child A is enrolled in both the Main Literacy Programme and Maths Programme and is receiving a bursary. Child A is entitled to receive a second SES bursary if he/she enrols in the Speech and Drama Arts Programme.&nbsp;</p></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2117" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="7" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2117" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">7. How often are classes conducted?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2117" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="7" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2117"><p style="font-weight: 400;">Each SDA class is 1.5 hours long, once a week. Our classes are only conducted on Saturdays at selected das Learning Centres.</p></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2118" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="8" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2118" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">

													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">8. Which DAS Learning Centre offer the SDA Programme?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2118" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="8" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2118"><p style="font-weight: 400;">Currently, the SDA programme is available at Bishan Learning Centre.</p></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-2119" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="9" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2119" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">9. What are our Placement Procedures?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2119" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="9" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2119"><p style="font-weight: 400;">Parents may submit an application through the das website&nbsp;<a href="https://eportal.das.org.sg/das/maf_new">here</a>. Once the application has been processed, the Programme Manager or SDA Teacher will contact the parent to discuss and find a suitable class for the child.</p></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-21110" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="10" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-21110" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">10. What is your teaching approach? </a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-21110" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="10" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-21110"><p style="font-weight: 400;">We use the Orton-Gillingham Approach.</p><ol><li style="font-weight: 400;">Language-based – Exposure to different texts to enhance students’ appreciation of the English language through Drama.</li><li style="font-weight: 400;">Cognitive-&nbsp; the activities are crafted to engage their cognition e.g. creative story writing, roleplay, improvisation, memorising scripts, rehearsing and performing with movements and cues&nbsp;</li><li style="font-weight: 400;">Structured, Sequential and Cumulative – includes direct and explicit instruction and has a different range of difficulty level for all activities&nbsp;</li><li style="font-weight: 400;">Simultaneous multi-sensory – engage through stage and hand props, presentation of skills through multiple senses, eg. Using visual and aural cues</li><li style="font-weight: 400;">Diagnostic-prescriptive – Drama Instructors regularly assess students’ abilities and adapt activities according to the class dynamics.</li><li style="font-weight: 400;">Emotionally sound – Drama Instructors are trained in the special needs field who have a better understanding of our students’ needs and strengths.</li></ol></div>
				</div>
							<div class="elementor-toggle-item">
					<div id="elementor-tab-title-21111" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="11" role="button" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-21111" aria-expanded="false">
												<span class="elementor-toggle-icon elementor-toggle-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
															<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-closed"><i class="fas fa-caret-right"></i></span>
								<span class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened"><i class="elementor-toggle-icon-opened fas fa-caret-up"></i></span>
													</span>
												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">11. My child has dyslexia but is not a student at DAS. Can he still enrol into the programme?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-21111" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="11" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-21111"><p>The SDA Programme is open to both non-DAS students and DAS students. No formal diagnosis of dyslexia is required.</p><p><strong>Call 6444 5700 for more information.</strong></p></div>
				</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
window.addEventListener("load", function(event) {
jQuery(".cfx_form_main,.wpcf7-form,.wpforms-form,.gform_wrapper form").each(function(){
var form=jQuery(this); 
var screen_width=""; var screen_height="";
 if(screen_width == ""){
 if(screen){
   screen_width=screen.width;  
 }else{
     screen_width=jQuery(window).width();
 }    }  
  if(screen_height == ""){
 if(screen){
   screen_height=screen.height;  
 }else{
     screen_height=jQuery(window).height();
 }    }
form.append('<input type="hidden" name="vx_width" value="'+screen_width+'">');
form.append('<input type="hidden" name="vx_height" value="'+screen_height+'">');
form.append('<input type="hidden" name="vx_url" value="'+window.location.href+'">');  
}); 

});
</script> 
<script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(window).scroll(function() {    
        var scroll = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
        if (scroll >= 400) {
            jQuery("#header").addClass("fixed-header");
        } else {
            jQuery("#header").removeClass("fixed-header");
        }
    });
    jQuery('.get-in-touch-menu.elementor-widget-nav-menu ul .search-menus').on( "click", function() {
        jQuery('#header .search-menu .elementor-search-form__toggle i').click();
    });
    jQuery('#header .premium-toggle-text').click(function(e) {
     e.preventDefault();
     jQuery("#close-filter").remove();
     jQuery(".premium-mobile-menu-container").prepend('<i id="close-filter" class="fa fa-times"></i>');
 });
    jQuery('body').on('click', '#close-filter', function() {
     jQuery("#header .premium-toggle-close").trigger('click'); 
 });
